# Project Status

Last updated: 2026-04-27 by Claude (**Printable Refresher (PRF) — PRF-G5-UI continuing — S26 adds A4 page-size visual regression baselines. 3 new Playwright tests pre-seeding `pageSize='a4'` via existing `setPrintPrefs` helper + 9 new baseline PNGs (3 tests × 3 browsers). Directory total: 30 baselines = 10 snapshot tests × 3 browsers. All 33 test runs (11 tests × 3 browsers) green; 3.2m wall time on stable second run.** Continues PRF-G5-UI from S18+S19+S20+S21+S22+S23+S24+S25. **S26 deliverables (1 file edit + 9 new baseline PNGs):** **(1)** `tests/playwright/printable-refresher.spec.js` MODIFIED — 3 new tests added after the existing PrintPreview Letter variants: "PrintPreview — 12-up A4 Color" / "PrintPreview — 4-up A4 Color" / "PrintPreview — 1-up A4 B&W". Each pre-seeds `pageSize='a4'` (plus the corresponding cardsPerSheet + colorMode) via the existing `setPrintPrefs(page, prefs)` helper before navigation, so PrintPreview hydrates with the desired layout. Snapshot scope mirrors the Letter variants: `.print-preview-container` for 12-up + 4-up; first `.refresher-print-page` only for 1-up (1-up output spans 6 pages; one page is enough to validate the layout class). Doc-comment correction: original comment said "body[data-page-size]" but the actual CSS selector is `.print-preview-container[data-page-size]` — fixed inline. **(2)** `tests/playwright/printable-refresher.spec.js-snapshots/` — 9 new baseline PNGs: print-preview-12up-a4-color × {chromium,firefox,webkit}, print-preview-4up-a4-color × 3, print-preview-1up-a4-bw-page1 × 3. Total directory now 30 baselines = 10 snapshot tests × 3 browsers (the 11th test "end-to-end: enable staleness in Settings → banner appears in Refresher" is behavior-only with no snapshot). **All 33 test runs (11 tests × 3 browsers) green on first generation pass (~1.8m)** + green again on stable second run (3.2m wall time, faster than S25's 7.1m because dev-server stays warm across more tests per run-pass — per-test cost was offset by per-spawn fixed cost spreading over 33 runs vs 24). **Per-page-size observations:** A4 baselines are slightly larger file size than Letter at the same grid mode (more vertical pixels because row heights are taller — e.g. 12-up A4 chromium = 120 KB vs 12-up Letter chromium = 113 KB; 1-up A4 B&W = 39 KB vs 1-up Letter B&W = 38 KB). Visually, the row-height difference is subtle (2.25→2.4in for 12-up = 6.7% increase) but real layout regressions in the A4 variant would now be caught by the snapshot diff. The CSS selector `.print-preview-container[data-page-size="a4"] .refresher-print-page[data-cards-per-sheet="N"]` correctly applies compressed row heights for A4's 11.69" page (vs Letter's 11"). **Doctrine choices established this session:** (a) **Letter + A4 only, not the full 4 grid modes × 2 page sizes = 8** — 3 representative A4 variants (12-up + 4-up + 1-up; skip 6-up since 12-up already covers the most common case) keep snapshot count manageable. Future sessions can add 6-up A4 if owner-visible regressions surface. (b) **Reuse `setPrintPrefs` helper from S23** — pre-seeds IDB with the page-size + grid-size + color-mode in a single call. No new helper functions; the pattern is already established. The same helper handles `pageSize` even though it wasn't exercised before S26 — flexibility designed in from the start, paying off here. (c) **Cross-browser pass on the A4 variants** — same per-project thresholds apply (chromium strict / firefox 0.25 / webkit 0.3); A4 row-height difference doesn't require additional tuning since the rendering jitter sources are the same. (d) **A4 1-up snapshots first page only** — same convention as Letter 1-up (the 1-up output spans 6 pages; one is enough to validate the `data-cards-per-sheet="1"` class + first-page rendering; full 6-page snapshots would balloon storage with diminishing visual-regression value). (e) **Doc-comment hygiene** — caught + fixed an inline reference to `body[data-page-size]` that was incorrect (actual selector is `.print-preview-container[data-page-size]`). Worth keeping spec doc-comments accurate as they're future test-author reference. **Phase 5 status post-S26:** PRF-G5-CI ✓ + MIG ✓ + SL+ST ✓ + WR ✓ + HK ✓ + RL+RI+DS+LG ✓ + AppRoot wiring ✓ + PRF-G5-B 6-of-6 cards ✓ + PRF-G5-UI shell + 4 card templates + sub-views + PrintPreview + PrintControls + PrintConfirmationModal + global stylesheet + StalenessBanner + Settings staleness toggle + PRF-G5-PDF Playwright baseline + cross-browser baselines + **A4 page-size baselines** ✓ (S18+S19+S20+S21+S22+S23+S24+S25+S26). **NEXT (S27+):** owner priority pick from: (a) `data-include-lineage="off"` snapshot variant (currently only `on`; covers the lineage-toggle off state across browsers; ~3 new snapshots × 3 browsers = 9 baselines); (b) SuppressConfirmModal + LineageModal snapshots (already unit-tested but visual regression would catch CSS drift; ~6 baselines); (c) CardDetail snapshots per class (only math has manifests today; preflop/equity/exceptions gated on Phase A/C card authoring); (d) URL routing for sub-views (`#printableRefresher/card/PRF-X` deep-links open CardDetail; same pattern for `/print-preview`); (e) Filter expansion (phases + tiers in addition to classes); (f) 16-permutation full grid×page×color matrix; (g) CI integration (Playwright config has `forbidOnly: !!process.env.CI` ready; needs a CI workflow file); (h) PRF-G5-A Phase A preflop card authoring (Q5 differentiation demo first); (i) PRF-G5-C Phase C equity + exceptions card authoring. **Parallel-session coordination:** S26 owned `tests/playwright/printable-refresher.spec.js` (3 tests appended) + 9 new baseline PNGs. **Prior update (superseded, kept for provenance — 2026-04-27 PRF S25):** (**Printable Refresher (PRF) — PRF-G5-UI continuing — S25 extends visual regression coverage from chromium-only to chromium + firefox + webkit (3-browser baselines). 14 new baseline PNGs (7 firefox + 7 webkit) added to existing 7 chromium baselines — directory total: 21 baselines = 7 snapshot tests × 3 browsers. All 24 test runs (8 tests × 3 browsers) stable on second run (7.1m wall time). Per-project threshold tuning: chromium strict (maxDiffPixels: 100, threshold: 0.2); firefox relaxed (800, 0.25); webkit most relaxed (1200, 0.3) to absorb genuine cross-browser font/antialiasing jitter without false positives.** Continues PRF-G5-UI from S18+S19+S20+S21+S22+S23+S24. **S25 deliverables:** **(1) Browser-binary install** — `npx playwright install firefox webkit` installed firefox v148 (113 MB) + webkit v26.4 (58 MB) under `~/.cache/ms-playwright/`. Chromium was already cached from S23. **(2)** `playwright.config.js` MODIFIED — `projects` array extended from 1 entry to 3 entries (chromium / firefox / webkit). All 3 projects share the same Galaxy A22 1600×720 viewport per CLAUDE.md mobile target. Per-project `expect.toHaveScreenshot` overrides relax thresholds for firefox + webkit: chromium keeps the strict default (`maxDiffPixels: 100, threshold: 0.2`); firefox uses `{ maxDiffPixels: 800, threshold: 0.25 }` to absorb font-hinting + subpixel positioning differences from chromium at A22 viewport (visible most in card body paragraphs); webkit uses `{ maxDiffPixels: 1200, threshold: 0.3 }` for the largest jitter — webkit on Windows has font fallback (no Georgia available; falls back to system serif) + antialiasing differences vs chromium/firefox. All 3 share the same `webServer` auto-spawn + `fullyParallel: false` + `workers: 1` (single dev server + single IDB; parallel would race on state). **(3)** `tests/playwright/printable-refresher.spec.js-snapshots/` — 14 new baseline PNGs (7 firefox-suffixed + 7 webkit-suffixed) committed. Directory total: 21 baselines = 7 snapshot tests (catalog-default / catalog-staleness-banner / print-confirmation-modal / print-preview-12up-letter-color / print-preview-1up-letter-bw-page1 / print-preview-4up-letter-color / settings-refresher-section) × 3 browsers (chromium / firefox / webkit). The 8th test ("end-to-end: enable staleness in Settings → banner appears in Refresher") is behavior-only with no snapshot. **All 24 test runs (8 tests × 3 browsers) green on first generation pass + green again on stable second run (7.1m wall time including dev-server startup once per browser project).** **Per-browser observations** captured for future-session reference: firefox renders fonts with slightly heavier weight + tighter letter-spacing vs chromium; webkit uses a different fallback font on Windows (Georgia not available); the `linear-gradient(to top, accent X%, transparent)` mixed-frequency cell rendering used in PreflopCardTemplate works identically across all 3 browsers (relevant for future Phase A card snapshots); the PrintConfirmationModal date-input mask works identically across all 3 browsers. **Doctrine choices established this session:** (a) **Per-project threshold tuning, not global** — chromium stays at the strict default; firefox + webkit get relaxed defaults. This keeps chromium as the gold-standard regression detector while accommodating genuine cross-browser jitter without false positives. If a real layout regression slips past firefox/webkit but is caught by chromium, that's the safety net working as designed. (b) **A22 viewport across all 3 projects** — could have used Desktop Firefox / Desktop Safari default viewports but consistency matters more for layout-equivalence verification across browsers. (c) **No webkit-specific reference cards yet** — the per-class accent colors (navy / burnt-orange / teal / maroon) all render acceptably across browsers; if webkit's font fallback ever produces a regression that chromium misses, we'd add a webkit-only assertion then. Premature optimization to add separate reference paths now. (d) **Test execution time grew from 8s → 7.1m** — webServer spawns once per project (3 spawns total), each adding ~1m server-boot overhead. Acceptable trade-off for cross-browser coverage; can be parallelized later via `workers: 3` if it becomes a CI bottleneck (would require dev-server-per-worker isolation, deferred). (e) **firefox + webkit baselines ARE tracked content** — the existing `!tests/playwright/**/*.png` exception in `.gitignore` (added in S23) covers all baselines regardless of browser. No gitignore changes needed in S25. (f) **Webkit baselines fail more gracefully on Windows** — webkit on Windows is a Playwright build (not Safari proper), so font availability differs from real Safari. Tests run + assert layout equivalence; a real "Safari user" test would need a macOS or Linux runner. Acceptable for visual regression of the layout/CSS contract; not a substitute for real-Safari user testing. **Phase 5 status post-S25:** PRF-G5-CI ✓ + MIG ✓ + SL+ST ✓ + WR ✓ + HK ✓ + RL+RI+DS+LG ✓ + AppRoot wiring ✓ + PRF-G5-B 6-of-6 cards ✓ + PRF-G5-UI shell + 4 card templates + sub-views + PrintPreview + PrintControls + PrintConfirmationModal + global stylesheet + StalenessBanner + Settings staleness toggle + PRF-G5-PDF Playwright baseline + **cross-browser baselines** ✓ (S18+S19+S20+S21+S22+S23+S24+S25). **NEXT (S26+):** owner priority pick from: (a) A4 page-size baselines (currently only Letter snapshotted across all 3 browsers; A4 grids differ at 12-up/6-up); (b) CardDetail snapshots per class (only math has manifests today; preflop/equity/exceptions gated on Phase A/C card authoring); (c) URL routing for sub-views (`#printableRefresher/card/PRF-X` deep-links open CardDetail; same pattern for `/print-preview`); (d) Filter expansion (phases + tiers in addition to classes); (e) 16-permutation full grid×page×color matrix; (f) `data-include-lineage="off"` snapshot variant; (g) SuppressConfirmModal + LineageModal snapshots; (h) CI integration (Playwright config has `forbidOnly: !!process.env.CI` ready; needs a CI workflow file); (i) PRF-G5-A Phase A preflop card authoring (Q5 differentiation demo first); (j) PRF-G5-C Phase C equity + exceptions card authoring. **Parallel-session coordination:** S25 owned `playwright.config.js` (extended from 1 to 3 projects; minor doc-comment update) + 14 new baseline PNGs in `tests/playwright/printable-refresher.spec.js-snapshots/`. No source code changes. EAL S15-S17 + parallel sessions in `src/hooks/`, `src/contexts/`, `src/components/views/HandReplayView/` are untouched. PokerTracker.jsx + AppProviders.jsx + useAppState.js untouched. **Prior update (superseded, kept for provenance — 2026-04-27 PRF S24):** (**Printable Refresher (PRF) — PRF-G5-UI continuing — S24 ships Settings staleness toggle, unblocking the AP-PRF-08-gated S22 StalenessBanner for production. New `RefresherSettings.jsx` section in SettingsView with Off/On toggle wired to `refresher.patchConfig({ notifications: { staleness } })`. End-to-end Playwright e2e test verifies the full flow: pre-seed stale batch → banner hidden by default → navigate to Settings via hash → click On → navigate back to Refresher → banner appears. 8/8 Playwright baselines stable; 12/12 RefresherSettings unit tests green; 240/240 PRF view-scope tests unchanged. Real bug caught + fixed by Playwright e2e: Refresher view hides the sidebar so the e2e test couldn't click "Settings" from there — fixed by using `window.location.hash = '#settings'` + `page.reload()` (set hash BEFORE reload). Pattern documented for future cross-view e2e tests.** Continues PRF-G5-UI from S18+S19+S20+S21+S22+S23. **S24 deliverables (1 new component + 1 new test file + 2 file edits + extended Playwright spec + 1 new snapshot):** **(1)** `src/components/views/SettingsView/RefresherSettings.jsx` (NEW, ~80 LOC) — new "Printable Refresher" section in the Settings 2-column grid. Single toggle: "Show staleness banner" with Off/On buttons (Tailwind, GOLD heading per existing section pattern). aria-pressed reflects current `notifications.staleness` value; ≥44px tap targets per H-ML06 via `min-h-[44px]` Tailwind utility. Pending-flag guards rapid double-clicks (only the first click dispatches while a write is in-flight). Calls `refresher.patchConfig({ notifications: { staleness: bool } })` (W-URC-1) on click; surfaces writer-rejection inline as `role="alert"` (red styling). `data-testid="refresher-settings-section"` for CI introspection. Factual explainer copy ("Surface a banner in the Printable Refresher when printed cards have changed since you last printed them. Default is off.") per CD-1; no engagement / no nag pattern. **(2)** `src/components/views/SettingsView/SettingsView.jsx` MODIFIED — imports + mounts `<RefresherSettings />` between `<DataAndAbout />` and `<ErrorLogPanel />` in the existing 2-col grid. No prop threading needed; component composes `useRefresher()` directly. **(3)** `src/components/views/SettingsView/__tests__/RefresherSettings.test.jsx` (NEW, 12 tests): render — heading + label + explainer / Off+On buttons in `<div role="group" aria-label="Staleness banner toggle">` / `data-testid` attribute / aria-pressed reflects state (Off-default + On-when-true + Off-default-when-notifications-field-missing); accessibility — Tailwind `min-h-[44px]` class on all buttons (jsdom doesn't compute Tailwind to inline styles so test inspects className regex); patchConfig wiring — clicking On dispatches `patchConfig({ notifications: { staleness: true } })` + clicking Off dispatches inverse + rapid double-click safely guarded by pending flag (only first call dispatches; second is no-op while in-flight) + writer rejection surfaces inline as role=alert. **All 12/12 green.** PRF view-scope unchanged at 240/15 (S24 work is in SettingsView/, not PrintableRefresherView/). **(4)** `tests/playwright/printable-refresher.spec.js` extended (+2 tests, +1 new snapshot baseline `settings-refresher-section-chromium-win32.png`): "Settings — Refresher section visible (S24)" snapshots the section card via `[data-testid="refresher-settings-section"]` locator after navigation via hash deep-link; "end-to-end: enable staleness in Settings → banner appears in Refresher (S24)" exercises the full flow: pre-seed stale batch via `page.evaluate` IDB write → navigate to Refresher via hash → confirm banner hidden by default (AP-PRF-08 OFF) → navigate to Settings via `window.location.hash = '#settings'` + `page.reload()` → click On → verify aria-pressed flips → navigate back to Refresher via hash → assert `.refresher-staleness-banner` becomes visible. **All 8/8 Playwright snapshots stable on second run (9.5s).** **Real bug caught + fixed by Playwright:** initial e2e test used sidebar `getByRole('button', { name: 'Settings' }).click()` to navigate from Refresher to Settings — failed because the Refresher view hides the CollapsibleSidebar (it's a full-screen view with its own header + back button; sidebar is Table-view-only). Failure screenshot showed Refresher catalog rendered with PRF-MATH-AUTO-PROFIT marked Stale (because the seed worked) but no sidebar to click. Fix: use `window.location.hash = '#settings'` + `page.reload()` — set hash BEFORE reload so React's `useEffect` HASH_TO_SCREEN handler reads it on fresh mount. Documented inline in the e2e test for future cross-view test reference. **Doctrine choices established this session:** (a) **Toggle gated at writer level, not component level** — `notifications.staleness` value passes through `patchConfig({ notifications })` to W-URC-1 which validates the nested key. Component just calls the writer; writer enforces. Defense-in-depth without UI-level validation duplication. Mirrors the PrintControls pattern. (b) **No debounce on settings-toggle writes** — settings toggles are owner-deliberate, single-click actions. Unlike PrintControls (which can fire 4+ toggles in rapid succession via owner cycling through grid/page/color/lineage), settings rarely sees rapid changes. Pending-flag guards double-click; that's the only protection needed. Fewer moving parts. (c) **Mount in 2-col grid between DataAndAbout and ErrorLogPanel** — no semantic ordering rationale; just a visually-balanced position in the existing layout. Owner can find it scrolling the Settings page. Could promote to a more prominent position (e.g. just under DisplaySettings) once Phase 5 has more refresher-related toggles to group. (d) **Hash-deep-link for cross-view test navigation** — when the destination view hides the sidebar (like Refresher → Settings), use `window.location.hash = '#hash'` + `page.reload()`. Set hash BEFORE reload (otherwise the useEffect-on-mount has nothing to read). Pattern reusable for any cross-view e2e tests. (e) **Tailwind class regex for tap-target tests** — jsdom doesn't compute Tailwind to inline styles, so the test inspects `b.className` for `/min-h-\[44px\]/` rather than `getComputedStyle().minHeight`. Pattern reusable for any Tailwind-only-styled component. **Phase 5 status post-S24:** PRF-G5-CI ✓ + MIG ✓ + SL+ST ✓ + WR ✓ + HK ✓ + RL+RI+DS+LG ✓ + AppRoot wiring ✓ + PRF-G5-B 6-of-6 cards ✓ + PRF-G5-UI shell + 4 card templates + sub-views + PrintPreview + PrintControls + PrintConfirmationModal + global stylesheet + StalenessBanner + PRF-G5-PDF Playwright baseline + **Settings staleness toggle** ✓ (S18+S19+S20+S21+S22+S23+S24). The S22 StalenessBanner is now reachable in production by any owner who clicks Settings → Printable Refresher → On. **NEXT (S25+):** owner priority pick from: (a) Cross-browser baselines (firefox + webkit per snapshot = 24 baselines total now); (b) A4 page-size variants (currently only Letter snapshotted); (c) CardDetail snapshots per class (only math has manifests today; others gated on Phase A/C card authoring); (d) URL routing for sub-views (`#printableRefresher/card/PRF-X` deep-links open CardDetail); (e) Filter expansion (phases + tiers in addition to classes); (f) PRF-G5-A Phase A preflop card authoring (Q5 differentiation demo first); (g) PRF-G5-C Phase C equity + exceptions card authoring. **Parallel-session coordination:** S24 owned `src/components/views/SettingsView/RefresherSettings.jsx` (new) + `SettingsView.jsx` (1 import + 1 component mount) + `__tests__/RefresherSettings.test.jsx` (new) + `tests/playwright/printable-refresher.spec.js` (extended) + 1 new snapshot baseline. EAL S15-S17 + parallel sessions in `src/hooks/`, `src/contexts/`, `src/components/views/HandReplayView/` are untouched. PokerTracker.jsx + AppProviders.jsx + useAppState.js untouched. Top-entry succession: EAL S14 → PRF S20 → EAL S15 → EAL S16 → EAL S17 → PRF S21 → EAL S17 visual-verification → PRF S22 → PRF S23 → PRF S24 (this entry). Handoff: `.claude/handoffs/printable-refresher-session24.md`.)

**Prior update (superseded, kept for provenance — 2026-04-27 PRF S23):** (**Printable Refresher (PRF) — PRF-G5-UI continuing — S23 ships PRF-G5-PDF: Playwright visual regression infrastructure + 6-snapshot starter baseline (chromium, Galaxy A22 1600×720, Letter only). `@playwright/test` ^1.59.1 installed as devDep + chromium browser binary. `playwright.config.js` + `tests/playwright/printable-refresher.spec.js` + 3 npm scripts (`test:visual` / `test:visual:update` / `test:visual:debug`). 6 baselines captured + stable on second run (8s): catalog default / PrintPreview 12-up Letter Color / 4-up Letter Color / 1-up Letter B&W page-1 / PrintConfirmationModal (date-input masked) / catalog with StalenessBanner visible after IDB seed. CI bundle-grep gate passes; visual baselines committed to repo as visual-regression source-of-truth (`!tests/playwright/**/*.png` gitignore exception); per-run artifacts ignored. Real bug caught + fixed by Playwright: hash-deep-link navigation pattern doesn't re-fire React's `useEffect`, so `gotoRefresher` rewritten to `page.reload()` + sidebar-button click. Cross-browser (firefox + webkit) + A4 grids + CardDetail per-class + full 16-permutation matrix all deferred to S24+.** Continues PRF-G5-UI from S18+S19+S20+S21+S22. **S23 deliverables:** **(1)** `package.json` MODIFIED — added `@playwright/test ^1.59.1` devDep + 3 npm scripts: `test:visual` (run + compare baselines), `test:visual:update` (regenerate after intentional UI changes), `test:visual:debug` (headed run). Chromium browser binary installed via `npx playwright install chromium`. **(2)** `playwright.config.js` (NEW) — chromium project (firefox/webkit deferred), Galaxy A22 1600×720 viewport per CLAUDE.md mobile target, port 5193 with `--strictPort`, `webServer` auto-spawns `npm run dev`, `fullyParallel: false` + `workers: 1` (single dev server + single IDB; parallel would race on state). `expect.toHaveScreenshot` defaults: `maxDiffPixels: 100`, `threshold: 0.2`, `animations: disabled`. Output dir `tests/playwright/.test-results/` (gitignored). `forbidOnly: !!process.env.CI` ready for future CI workflow. **(3)** `tests/playwright/printable-refresher.spec.js` (NEW) — 6-snapshot starter baseline + documented helper pattern for S24+ extension. Helpers: `resetRefresherIDB(page)` wipes printBatches + resets config to sensible defaults via `page.evaluate()` IDB manipulation; `setPrintPrefs(page, prefs)` patches `userRefresherConfig.printPreferences` directly so PrintPreview hydrates with desired layout (faster + less flaky than driving toggle UI); `seedStaleScenario(page)` flips `notifications.staleness=true` + inserts a stub `printBatch` with diverging contentHashes (mirrors S22 visual-verification pattern); `gotoRefresher(page)` does `page.reload()` + clicks sidebar Refresher button (deep-link via `page.goto('/#hash')` doesn't re-trigger React's `useEffect` on Playwright's same-origin nav so the click pattern is more reliable — fixed during baseline-generation when all 6 tests timed out waiting for "Print preview →"). 6 snapshots: catalog default 6 math cards + PrintPreview 12-up Letter Color (all 6 on 1 page) + PrintPreview 4-up Letter Color (6 across 2 pages) + PrintPreview 1-up Letter B&W page-1 only + PrintConfirmationModal opened on top of PrintPreview (with date-input masked via `mask: [dialog.getByLabel('Print date')]` so baseline doesn't drift daily) + catalog with StalenessBanner visible after IDB seed. **(4)** `tests/playwright/printable-refresher.spec.js-snapshots/` (NEW directory) — 6 baseline PNGs (450 KB total) committed to repo: `catalog-default-chromium-win32.png` (76 KB), `catalog-staleness-banner-chromium-win32.png` (81 KB), `print-confirmation-modal-chromium-win32.png` (29 KB), `print-preview-12up-letter-color-chromium-win32.png` (113 KB), `print-preview-1up-letter-bw-page1-chromium-win32.png` (38 KB), `print-preview-4up-letter-color-chromium-win32.png` (126 KB). All baselines stable on second run with no flag (8.0s). **(5)** `.gitignore` MODIFIED — added `tests/playwright/.test-results/` + `playwright-report/` + `test-results/` to ignore per-run artifacts; added `!tests/playwright/**/*.png` exception so snapshot baselines ARE tracked (visual regression source-of-truth; the existing `*.png` rule would have ignored them otherwise). **All 6 baselines stable on second run; CI bundle-grep gate passes ✓.** **Real bug caught + fixed by Playwright:** initial spec used `page.goto('/#printableRefresher')` for navigation, but Playwright treats hash-only changes on same-origin SPA as a no-op for `useEffect` re-fires, so the HASH_TO_SCREEN handler in `PokerTracker.jsx` didn't route to the catalog. All 6 tests timed out waiting for "Print preview →" (failure screenshot showed Table view rendered instead of Refresher). Fix: rewrote `gotoRefresher` to `page.reload()` + `page.click('button:has-text("Refresher")')` — mirrors how an owner navigates + always works deterministically. Documented in spec doc-comment for future session reference. **Doctrine choices established this session:** (a) **IDB seeding via `page.evaluate`, not UI clicks** — for state-dependent snapshots (banner-visible, custom prefs), seeding directly into IDB before navigation is faster + less flaky than driving toggle UI sequences. Pattern documented in spec helpers; reusable for any opt-in-gated or persistence-backed feature. (b) **Region-targeted screenshots, not full viewport** — `expect(page.getByRole('main')).toHaveScreenshot()` and `expect(page.locator('.print-preview-container')).toHaveScreenshot()` keep baselines tight against scroll-position + browser-chrome drift. Full-viewport snapshots reserved for whole-page regression checks. (c) **Date-input masking** in PrintConfirmationModal snapshot — `mask: [dialog.getByLabel('Print date')]` paints a uniform overlay so today's-date drift doesn't flake the baseline daily. Pattern reusable for any time-dependent UI (relative timestamps, "just now" labels, etc.). (d) **Cross-browser deferred to S24+** — chromium-only baseline ships first since chromium has the most reliable `@page` CSS support + fastest iteration. Firefox + webkit regression coverage when there's evidence of browser-specific rendering divergence (so far there isn't). (e) **`fullyParallel: false` + `workers: 1`** — single dev server + IDB; parallel workers would race on IDB state. Trade-off: slower test runs (8s for 6 snapshots) for deterministic state. (f) **Hash-deep-link unreliable in Playwright** — `page.goto('/#fragment')` on a same-origin SPA doesn't re-trigger React's mount-time `useEffect`. Use `page.reload()` + UI click for navigation. Documented in spec doc-comment so future test authors don't repeat the trap. (g) **Reload-before-each pattern** — every test starts with `resetRefresherIDB` (which itself does a `page.goto('/')` for IDB access) followed by `gotoRefresher` (which does another `page.reload()`). Two reloads per test feels redundant but preserves clean IDB state without `beforeAll` setup complexity. (h) **Visual regression baselines ARE tracked content** — the `!tests/playwright/**/*.png` exception in `.gitignore` is intentional. The PNGs are the source-of-truth; without them the test infrastructure can't compare. Per-run output (test-results/, playwright-report/) stays gitignored. **Phase 5 status post-S23:** PRF-G5-CI ✓ + MIG ✓ + SL+ST ✓ + WR ✓ + HK ✓ + RL+RI+DS+LG ✓ + AppRoot wiring ✓ + PRF-G5-B 6-of-6 cards ✓ + PRF-G5-UI shell + 4 card templates + sub-views CardDetail + LineageModal + SuppressConfirmModal + menu entry + PrintPreview + PrintControls + PrintConfirmationModal + global stylesheet + StalenessBanner + **PRF-G5-PDF Playwright snapshot baseline** ✓ (S18+S19+S20+S21+S22+S23). **NEXT (S24+):** owner priority pick from: (a) **Cross-browser baselines** — extend `playwright.config.js` projects to add firefox + webkit; regenerate baselines per-browser; ~3 baselines × 3 browsers = 18 PNGs. deleted 4 redundant template imports. **(10)** Tests: 4 new files + 1 extended (~70 net new tests). `ClassDispatchedTemplate.test.jsx` (7 tests): 4 valid classes route correctly / unknown class falls to default placeholder / null manifest returns null / runtime + compact props pass through. `PrintControls.test.jsx` (18 tests): renders 4 toggle groups + all option buttons + aria-pressed reflects state + disabled includeCodex with tooltip + clicking each option schedules patchConfig with the right payload after 400ms debounce + rapid changes collapse into a single call (delta-merged via pendingPatchRef) + clicking disabled codex no-ops + writer rejection surfaces inline as role=alert + ≥44px tap targets. `PrintPreview.test.jsx` (16 tests): heading + back button + summary + PrintControls panel + WYSIWYG wrapper + grid pages count + 14-card multi-page chunk + cards via dispatched template + grid `data-cards-per-sheet` attr + container data-page-size/data-color-mode/data-include-lineage attrs + 4-up reflow + empty-state + Send-to-dialog-disabled-empty + onBack handler + onRequestPrintConfirm payload + perCardSnapshots map shape + I-WR-6 1:1 cardIds-vs-snapshots contract. `PrintConfirmationModal.test.jsx` (23 tests): title + summary + singular/plural + date input today default + optional label placeholder + factual reminder copy + Cancel/Confirm buttons + Confirm enabled by default (no checkbox gate) + aria-modal/aria-labelledby + ≥44px tap targets on buttons + minHeight on date/label inputs + Cancel/Esc/backdrop-click fire onCancel + click-inside-dialog does NOT close + label/date input edit + Confirm calls onConfirm with `{printedAt, label}` + label whitespace-trimmed-to-null when empty + onConfirm rejection surfaces error inline + "Recording…" submit state + Confirm disabled when printedAt empty + null-context fallback to 0/0. `PrintableRefresherView.test.jsx` extended (+6 tests; replaced footer-placeholder assertion): "Print preview →" entry-point + opens PrintPreview / Back returns to catalog / "Send to print dialog →" opens PrintConfirmationModal / Cancel returns to PrintPreview without firing recordPrintBatch / "Showing N of M" hidden in print-preview / entry-point hidden in print-preview. **All 215/215 PRF view-scope tests green across 14 files (was 145/10 at S20 baseline; +70 tests / +4 files); full PRF + persistence + reducer + hooks + context + UI scope 784/784 green across 30 test files** in isolation. CI bundle-grep gate (`scripts/check-refresher-bundle.sh`) passes — no html2canvas / jspdf / pdf-lib in PRF namespace. **Visual verification via Playwright (mandatory per session memory of S19 finding 2 browser-only bugs):** loaded `#printableRefresher` → catalog renders 6 math cards; clicked "Print preview →" → PrintPreview renders with 6 cards · 1 page on 12-up Letter Color (auto); toggled to 4-up → grid reflows to 6 cards · 2 pages with the IDB-persisted preference applied across reload; clicked "Send to print dialog →" → PrintConfirmationModal opens with summary "6 cards across 2 pages on Letter at 4-up (Color (auto))" + today's date prefilled + optional label + factual reminders + enabled Confirm button; pressed Esc → modal closes back to PrintPreview. **Zero console errors throughout the full flow.** Real browser-runtime bug caught + fixed: PrintControls' toggle buttons emitted React "Removing border borderColor" rerender warnings because `border` shorthand mixed with `borderColor` longhand across active/default state transitions. Fixed by switching to longhand-only `borderWidth/borderStyle/borderColor` triple. Fresh-tab reload after fix: 0 errors confirmed. **Doctrine choices established this session:** (a) **Lifted `ClassDispatchedTemplate` rather than duplicate** — two consumers (CardDetail + PrintPreview) is the minimum threshold for extraction; preserves single-source-of-truth for the 4-way dispatch. (b) **WYSIWYG via `.print-preview-container` global selector** — `@media print { ... }` and `.print-preview-container { ... }` blocks duplicate their bodies because CSS doesn't allow combining `@media` + class selectors; the duplication is intentional and small. On-screen preview matches printed output exactly without two-mode rendering. (c) **PrintConfirmationModal is NOT a 2-tap checkbox modal** — Suppress requires friction (R-8.1 zero-data-loss). Print is a normal owner action; immediate Confirm enabled. The print modal mirrors LineageModal's close behavior, not SuppressConfirmModal's gate behavior. (d) **printPreferences are IDB-persisted, not localStorage-only** — they survive cross-device sync via `userRefresherConfig` (W-URC-1). Distinct from `useRefresherView` (filter/sort) which is localStorage-only UI state. (e) **Native `<input type="date">` for printedAt** — no library; Galaxy A22 1600×720 mobile target gets the native picker; default value: today's YYYY-MM-DD via `todayIsoDate()` helper. (f) **Global stylesheet co-located with print rules, not component-scoped** — `@media print` rules don't reliably apply through component-style props; the `.print-preview-container` selector pattern requires global cascade. (g) **`window.print()` fires AFTER `await recordPrintBatch(payload)` resolves** — if the IDB write throws, the modal surfaces the error inline and `window.print()` does NOT fire. The writer promise is the sequencing guarantee — owner sees the failure before any browser dialog appears. (h) **Longhand-only border properties in PrintControls toggle buttons** — caught by Playwright as a React rerender warning when state toggled. The `borderWidth/borderStyle/borderColor` triple in the base style + `borderColor` override in the active style is consistent across all renders, eliminating the warning. Future inline-style toggles that change `borderColor` should follow this pattern. (i) **Pending-patch ref accumulator for debounce merge** — when 3 toggles fire within the 400ms window, the pending payload is merged in a `pendingPatchRef` and dispatched as a single `patchConfig` call, not 3 sequential calls. Mirrors EAL S15's `useAnchorObservationDraft` pattern. **Phase 5 status post-S21:** PRF-G5-CI ✓ + MIG ✓ + SL+ST ✓ + WR ✓ + HK ✓ + RL+RI+DS+LG ✓ + AppRoot wiring ✓ + PRF-G5-B 6-of-6 cards ✓ + PRF-G5-UI shell + 4 card templates + sub-views CardDetail + LineageModal + SuppressConfirmModal + menu entry + **PrintPreview + PrintControls + PrintConfirmationModal + global stylesheet** ✓ (S18+S19+S20+S21). **NEXT (S22+):** owner priority pick from: (a) StalenessBanner; (b) filter expansion (phases + tiers); (c) URL routing for sub-views; (d) PRF-G5-PDF Playwright snapshot baseline (now unblocked by S21); (e) PRF-G5-A Phase A preflop card authoring (Q5 differentiation demo); (f) PRF-G5-C Phase C equity + exceptions card authoring. **Parallel-session coordination:** S21 owned `PrintableRefresherView/*` + `src/styles/printable-refresher.css` + `src/constants/runtimeVersions.js` + `src/main.jsx` (1 import line). PokerTracker.jsx + AppProviders.jsx + useAppState.js untouched. Top-entry succession: EAL S14 → PRF S20 → EAL S15 → EAL S16 → EAL S17 → PRF S21 (this entry). **Prior update (superseded, kept for provenance — 2026-04-27 EAL S15):** (**Exploit Anchor Library (EAL) — Phase 6 Stream D B3 S15 — capture orchestrator hooks shipped (data layer for AnchorObservationModal complete).** Continues Phase 6 Stream D B3 from S14 (AppRoot wiring + e2e integration). Two new hooks compose the AnchorLibrary context + the S10 W-AO-1 pure writer (`captureObservation`) into the data-management layer that the S16 capture modal will consume directly. **S15 deliverables (2 new hook files + 2 new test files):** **(1)** `src/hooks/useAnchorObservationDraft.js` — per-hand draft sidecar. Reads existing draft via `selectDraftForHand(handId)`; exposes `updateDraft(partial)` that merges multiple rapid keystrokes into a single 400ms-debounced `DRAFT_UPDATED` dispatch (via a `pendingRef` that accumulates field-level partials, so a fast typer doesn't spam the reducer). `clearDraft()` dispatches `DRAFT_CLEARED` immediately + cancels any in-flight debounce — matters because Save and Discard both call `clearDraft` and a still-pending `DRAFT_UPDATED` would otherwise resurrect the draft after `clearDraft`. handId change cancels in-flight debounce (via cleanup effect); unmount cancels in-flight debounce. Defensive no-ops for empty handId / non-object partials. **(2)** `src/hooks/useAnchorObservationCapture.js` — orchestrator. Composes `useAnchorObservationDraft` + `useAnchorLibrary`. Manages local `isOpen` modal-visible state (openCapture / closeCapture). `save(input)` runs `captureObservation` pure-util with the global `enrollment.observation_enrollment_state` from context (drives I-WR-5 enrollment gate + I-WR-6 incognito honor); on `{ ok: true }`, dispatches `OBSERVATION_CAPTURED` + `DRAFT_CLEARED` as **two separate actions** (mirrors S12 capture-modal two-transaction discipline — persistence hook batches both writes within its 400ms cycle); returns the writer's `{ ok, record }` or `{ ok: false, errors }` for inline-error UI. `discard()` calls draft.clearDraft + closes modal (no `OBSERVATION_CAPTURED`). **closeCapture does NOT clear the draft** — that's the "Keep draft for later" implicit default; only the explicit-discard `discard()` path clears. Re-exports `draft / hasDraft / updateDraft` from the inner hook so the modal has one composed surface. **(3)** Tests (2 new files, 26 tests): useAnchorObservationDraft 14 tests (read path 3: null draft / existing draft / empty handId; updateDraft 6: no immediate dispatch / 400ms debounce dispatch / partials merged / debounce-reset on rapid updates / non-object defensive / empty-handId no-op; clearDraft 3: immediate dispatch / cancels-pending-update / empty-handId no-op; lifecycle 2: handId-change cancels pending / unmount cancels pending). useAnchorObservationCapture 12 tests (modal state 3: starts closed / openCapture / closeCapture-preserves-draft; save 6: ok-and-dispatches-both / I-WR-5-not-enrolled-forces-false / I-WR-6-incognito-honored / validation-errors-no-dispatch / missing-handId-error / observationIndex-deterministic-id; discard 1: clearDraft-and-close-no-dispatch; re-exports + enrollment 2: re-exports-from-inner-hook / isEnrolled-mirrors-context). **All 26/26 green; full EAL slice 469/469 green across 19 test files** (S14 baseline 443/17 → S15 469/19; +26 tests / +2 files). **Doctrine choices established this session:** (a) **Pending-merge ref over state-derived merge** — the debounced `updateDraft` accumulates partials in a ref, not by reading the latest state mid-debounce. This avoids races where multiple keystrokes within the debounce window each capture a different snapshot of state and the dispatch wins/loses depending on render timing. The ref is the canonical pending payload until the timer fires. (b) **clearDraft is non-debounced** — Save and Discard need DRAFT_CLEARED to propagate immediately so the persistence hook's diff-write picks it up on its next 400ms cycle without a still-pending DRAFT_UPDATED race-conditioning the wipe. (c) **Two-action save (not a fused action)** — saving dispatches OBSERVATION_CAPTURED then DRAFT_CLEARED separately. Mirrors S12 capture-modal two-transaction discipline. Worst-case partial-failure mode is a stale draft alongside a saved observation — next openCapture's resume-banner handles gracefully. (d) **closeCapture preserves draft** — surface spec specifies "Keep draft for later" as the implicit default for plain-close paths. Discard is a separate explicit action. The hook respects this asymmetry — closeCapture is non-destructive; only discard / save clear. (e) **Errors returned, not thrown** — captureObservation's validation errors are aggregated as a string array and returned to the modal so it can render them inline. Throwing would force consumers to wrap calls in try/catch. (f) **Mocked draft hook in orchestrator tests** — orchestrator tests mock `useAnchorObservationDraft` to focus on coordination; draft-hook behavior is verified in its own suite. Mirrors S13 pattern where context tests mocked the persistence hook. **Phase 6 Stream D B3 status post-S15:** S10 constants + capture pure-utils + observationTags ✓ + S11 v19 migration ✓ + S12 4-store wrappers ✓ + S13 reducer/context/persistence-hook ✓ + S14 AppRoot wiring + e2e integration ✓ + **S15 capture orchestrator hooks ✓** (data layer for the modal complete). **NEXT (S16):** AnchorObservationModal + AnchorObservationButton + AnchorObservationList — the 3 React components that compose `useAnchorObservationCapture` per surface spec. Modal needs 8-tag enum chip grid + custom-tag free-text input + street/action pickers + 280-char note + Incognito toggle (primary-visible per red line #9). Button is the ≥44×44 "🏷 Tag pattern" Section G entry. List renders existing observations chronological DESC. After S16: S17 wires Section G into HandReplayView ReviewPanel.jsx + visual verification at owner level. **Governance:** EAL Stream-D BACKLOG row updated with S15 deliverable detail. **Parallel session coordination:** PRF S20 prepended above me earlier in this session and owned only `PrintableRefresherView/*` files — no conflict with EAL's hook-only S15 scope. Top entry succession: EAL S14 → PRF S20 → EAL S15 (this entry). **Test status:** S15 net-add 26 tests across 2 new files. Full-suite check not run for S15 — same 14 parallel-session failures from S14 still expected (TelemetryConsent context missing test + migrationV21 timing-out + shape-language precisionAudit). Zero EAL regressions. Handoff: `.claude/handoffs/exploit-anchor-library-session15.md`.)

Region 2 renders 13×13 hand grid as a 169-cell CSS grid (`grid-template-columns: repeat(13, 1fr)`) generated from `manifest.generatedFields.rangeGrid` (169-entry frequency array per surface spec; `pokerCore/preflopCharts.js#computeOpenRange(position, stack, rake)` output shape). Region 3 derivation/exception callout (italic 9pt prose; second+ paragraphs from bodyMarkdown after `\n\n` split). Lineage footer + compact-mode mask gradient mirror MathCardTemplate exactly so all 4 templates share footer + compact behavior. Defensive: missing/non-array/wrong-length rangeGrid omits the entire grid (no crash); missing sizing omits sizing block; missing 2nd paragraph omits Region 3. **(2)** `src/components/views/PrintableRefresherView/EquityCardTemplate.jsx` — Phase C teal `#0f766e` accent template per surface spec §Template 3 (Equity). Region 2 renders the equity matrix as `<table role="table">` with `<th scope="col">` bucket headers from `generatedFields.equityMatrix.headers` + one `<tr>` per row in `equityMatrix.rows` with `<th scope="row">` texture name + cell percentages with `%` suffix and `font-variant-numeric: tabular-nums` for visual alignment. **Atomicity cap enforced at render-time**: rows sliced to ≤8 per H-PM05 (matches `equityMatrix` shape contract from surface spec; oversized matrix renders only first 8 rows — defense-in-depth for atomicity even if author authors a 12-row matrix). Region 3 bucket-definition citation (italicized 10pt prose from second+ bodyMarkdown paragraphs). Defensive: missing/non-array equityMatrix omits the table entirely. **(3)** `src/components/views/PrintableRefresherView/ExceptionsCardTemplate.jsx` — Phase C maroon `#7f1d1d` accent template per surface spec §Template 4 (Exceptions). Region 2 classifies bodyMarkdown paragraphs by **leading prefix** ("Solver baseline:" / "Live-pool divergence:" / "Override when:") into labeled sub-sections with accent-colored 9.5pt bold labels; unprefixed paragraphs fall through as plain prose. Region 3 hoists the override paragraph (if present) into a callout with light-red `#fef2f2` background + dashed top border + accent-colored "Override when:" label — visual emphasis on the override trigger per surface spec layout. Region 4-5 lineage footer additionally renders `audit id: <auditId>` line in accent color (the audit-id citation per F4 + F5 fidelity bar; auditId required for exceptions class per surface spec). Article also exposes `data-audit-id` HTML attribute for CI introspection (future content-drift CI test could grep for data-audit-id matches across exceptions cards to verify F4 attestation). Defensive: missing override paragraph omits Region 3 callout entirely; missing auditId omits the audit-id footer line + omits the data-audit-id attribute. Compact mode hides the entire footer + audit-id strip per consistent compact behavior across all 4 templates. **(4)** `src/components/views/PrintableRefresherView/CardDetail.jsx` MODIFIED — `ClassDispatchedTemplate` inner component upgraded from `if (manifest.class === 'math')` 1-of-1 dispatch with placeholder fallback to `switch (manifest.class)` 1-of-4 dispatch with `default` branch retaining the S19 placeholder for unknown classes. Imports added at top of file: `PreflopCardTemplate` / `EquityCardTemplate` / `ExceptionsCardTemplate` (MathCardTemplate import retained from S19). Zero coupling change to outer CardDetail — purely additive case branches in the inner dispatcher. **(5)** Tests: 3 new test files + 1 extended (49 net new tests). `PreflopCardTemplate.test.jsx` (16 tests): basic render: title 1 + navy accent #1e3a5f 1 + 169-cell grid render 1 + grid omits when rangeGrid missing or wrong-length 1 + sizing hint render 1 + Region 3 derivation 1 + Region 3 omits when no 2nd paragraph 1 + lineage footer render 1 + lineage compact-toggle 1 + null manifest returns null 1 + data-card-class attr 1 + data-card-id attr 1 + break-inside avoid 1 + grid aria-label 1 + data-cell labels (AA/AKs/AKo/22) 1 + mixed-frequency linear-gradient cell render 1. `EquityCardTemplate.test.jsx` (14 tests): title 1 + teal accent #0f766e 1 + table role 1 + column headers (Texture + 4 buckets) 1 + row headers (4 textures) 1 + cell percentages (3 unique values + 1 duplicate-count assertion) 1 + row cap at 8 per H-PM05 1 + table omits when matrix missing 1 + Region 3 bucket citation 1 + lineage compact-toggle 1 + null manifest 1 + data attrs 1 + break-inside avoid 1. `ExceptionsCardTemplate.test.jsx` (16 tests): title 1 + maroon accent #7f1d1d 1 + subtitle render 1 + "Solver baseline:" prefix classification 1 + "Live-pool divergence:" prefix classification 1 + "Override when:" hoisted to Region 3 1 + Region 3 omits when no override paragraph 1 + audit id in footer 1 + data-audit-id attr 1 + data-audit-id absent when undefined 1 + unprefixed-prose-fallback 1 + lineage compact-toggle hides audit-id 1 + null manifest 1 + data attrs 1 + break-inside avoid 1. `CardDetail.test.jsx` extended +3 net (replaced 1 placeholder-asserts-for-preflop with 4: dispatches preflop / dispatches equity / dispatches exceptions / unknown class falls back to placeholder). **All 145/145 view-scope tests green across 10 files (was 96/7 at S19 baseline; +49 tests / +3 files); full PRF + persistence + reducer + hooks + context + UI scope 714/714 green across 26 test files** in isolation. **Visual verification:** Math card detail still renders correctly through the new switch dispatcher (regression-verified via Playwright snapshot at `prf-s20-math-card-detail-regression.png`); zero console errors at boot or navigation. New 3 templates not yet visually verified at runtime because no preflop/equity/exceptions manifests exist yet — that work is gated on PRF-G5-A (Phase A preflop authoring) and PRF-G5-C (Phase C equity+exceptions authoring). Unit-test coverage substitutes for runtime verification until those phases ship. **Doctrine choices established this session:** (a) **All 4 templates share footer + compact behavior** — copying the lineage footer + mask-gradient block verbatim across templates (rather than extracting a shared `LineageFooter.jsx`) keeps the templates self-contained and easy to read at the cost of ~15 lines of duplication per template. The surface spec mentions `LineageFooter.jsx` as a future shared component; deferred until a 5th template arrives in Phase 2+ to motivate the extraction. (b) **`ClassDispatchedTemplate` migrated `if/else` → `switch` for clean 4-way + default branching** — `switch` makes the 4 valid classes + 1 defensive fallback explicit; future class additions are a single case branch + import. (c) **Default placeholder retained for defense-in-depth** — even with all 4 classes implemented, the default branch still renders the placeholder + `role="status"` so a corrupted manifest (typo in `manifest.class`) renders informatively rather than crashing. Tested explicitly with `class: 'unknown-class'`. (d) **Render-time atomicity cap on equity matrix** — surface spec H-PM05 says "row count ≤ 8"; rather than rejecting oversized matrices at the manifest validator level only, the template also slices to 8 rows at render time so even a malformed manifest renders within atomicity bounds. Defense-in-depth at the rendering layer. (e) **Exceptions template prefix-classifier is opportunistic, not mandatory** — paragraphs without recognized prefixes fall through as plain prose. The spec recommends specific section labels but the template doesn't crash when authors deviate; CI authoring tests can enforce prefix discipline at the manifest level if needed. (f) **`data-audit-id` HTML attribute on the article** — exposes the auditId for CI introspection without requiring DOM scraping of the footer text. Future `contentDrift.test.js` extension could grep `data-audit-id` matches across all exceptions cards to verify F4 attestation. (g) **Mixed-frequency cells use CSS `linear-gradient` not partial fills** — JSDOM renders gradients as a style string which tests can grep, and the gradient gives smoother visual intensity at print resolution than would alpha-channel fills (which can dither poorly on B&W laser printers per H-PM02). **Phase 5 status post-S20:** PRF-G5-CI ✓ + MIG ✓ + SL+ST ✓ + WR ✓ + HK ✓ + RL+RI+DS+LG ✓ + AppRoot wiring ✓ + PRF-G5-B 6-of-6 cards ✓ + PRF-G5-UI shell + 4 card templates + sub-views CardDetail + LineageModal + SuppressConfirmModal + menu entry ✓ (S18+S19+S20). **NEXT (S21):** Owner priority pick from: (a) PrintPreview sub-view + PrintConfirmationModal (W-URC-3 recordPrintBatch wired; needs grid layout per print-css-doctrine.md Region 1-6 + 4 grid modes × 2 page sizes × 2 color modes — most visible owner value + completes the print flow); (b) StalenessBanner (top-of-catalog count when `staleCardIds.size > 0`; selector already exposed via `useRefresher().getStaleCards()`); (c) filter expansion (phases + tiers in addition to classes; filter shape already supports them in useRefresherView state); (d) URL routing for sub-views (deep-link `#printableRefresher/card/PRF-X` opens detail directly); (e) PRF-G5-PDF Playwright cross-browser snapshots (4 grid × 2 page × 2 color = 16 per card × 6 math cards = 96-snapshot baseline). **Parallel-session coordination:** S20 owned `PrintableRefresherView/*` only — no shared-file edits. EAL S14's PokerTracker.jsx + AppProviders.jsx + useAppState.js + contexts/index.js edits are untouched. Handoff: `.claude/handoffs/printable-refresher-session20.md`.)

The unit-level persistence test mocks getAllPrimitives → empty, so this seeding path isn't exercised there. Worth knowing for the Phase 6+ Calibration Dashboard's "first-launch primitives panel" rendering. (b) **Reducer-state seeding is wiped by HYDRATED dispatch** — pre-populating `initialAnchorLibraryState.anchors` is meaningless because the persistence hook fires `ANCHOR_LIBRARY_HYDRATED` with empty IDB on first launch, replacing all 5 slices. Integration tests must seed via `putAnchor()` directly to IDB before mount, not via reducer state. (c) **Reducer merge contract holds across IDB round-trip** — `ANCHOR_OVERRIDDEN` payload `{id, status}` merged over the full pre-existing record + persisted as the merged record. Confirms the Phase 8 retirement orchestrator can dispatch partial-record overrides without losing fields. (d) **Auto-id-attachment on drafts is reducer-side, not wrapper-side** — DRAFT_UPDATED with `{handId: 'hand-int', partialNote: '...'}` (no id) gets `id: 'draft:hand-int'` from the reducer. The wrapper `putDraft()` would also auto-attach, but the reducer attaches first; both paths converge on the same id. **What this enables:** any view can now dispatch the 8 canonical actions safely; capture/library/calibration surfaces become buildable in Phase 6+. **Phase 6 Stream D B3 status post-S14:** S10 constants ✓ + S11 v19 migration ✓ + S12 4-store wrappers ✓ + S13 reducer/context/persistence-hook ✓ + S14 AppRoot wiring + e2e integration ✓. **NEXT (S15):** Surfaces — capture modal (HandReplayView Section G `hand-replay-observation-capture` surface) is the natural first surface to ship since it's the entry point for all owner-captured observations. Then `anchor-library` flat-list view, then `calibration-dashboard` study surface, then live-matcher integration in `LiveAdviceBar`. **Governance:** EAL Phase 6 Stream D B3 backlog row updated with S14 deliverable detail. Section header reflects "S14 — AppRoot wiring complete + integration test green." **Parallel session coordination:** Top entry succession went PRF S19 → EAL S14 (this entry). No file conflicts (PRF S19 owned PrintableRefresherView/* + CollapsibleSidebar.jsx; EAL S14 owns PokerTracker.jsx + useAppState.js + AppProviders.jsx + contexts/index.js + new contexts/__tests__/AnchorLibraryContext.integration.test.jsx). Promise.all over getRefresherConfig + getAllPrintBatches → single REFRESHER_HYDRATED dispatch; failure path dispatches with empty payload + still sets isReady true so app remains usable; cancellation guard via local cancelled flag prevents post-unmount dispatch. **(4)** `src/hooks/useRefresherView.js` — independent localStorage UI state (NO context coupling — UI state doesn't need to be in IDB-backed reducer). Hydrates from localStorage at key 'pokerTracker.refresherView.v1' on mount with defensive merge — coerces invalid sort values to default + non-array filter fields to [] + non-boolean showSuppressed to false via strict-equality `=== true` (rejects truthy non-boolean values like 'yes' which is friendlier than throwing but stricter than Boolean coercion). Persists synchronously on every change since localStorage is fast enough that debouncing would be over-engineering for non-load-bearing UI state. API: `{view, setFilter (partial-merge), setSort (enum-validated), setShowSuppressed (strict-equality), resetView}`. **(5)** `src/contexts/RefresherContext.jsx` — RefresherProvider receives state + dispatch + cardRegistry as deliberate inversion-of-control prop so tests can pass mock card sets; composes useRefresherPersistence; exposes 4 writer-action helpers `patchConfig` (W-URC-1 path — awaits writeConfigPreferences → dispatches REFRESHER_CONFIG_REPLACED with returned record) + `setCardVisibility` (W-URC-2a path) + `setClassSuppressed` (W-URC-2b path) + `recordPrintBatch` (W-URC-3 path — composes updatedConfig client-side from existing reducer state + new lastExportAt since W-URC-3 invokes W-URC-1 internally; client-side compose avoids re-reading IDB and gives single-dispatch atomicity at reducer level); 6 selector helpers `getAllCards` / `getActiveCards` / `getPinnedCards` / `getSuppressedCards` / `getCardsForBatchPrint` / `getStaleCards` via useCallback memoized over cardRegistry+config+printBatches; useRefresher consumer hook throws helpful error outside Provider. **(6)** `scripts/check-refresher-bundle.sh` — executable bash CI-grep gate per print-css-doctrine.md §Forbidden mechanisms; scans 7 PRF surface paths (`src/components/views/PrintableRefresherView/`, `src/utils/printableRefresher/`, `src/hooks/useRefresher*`, `src/contexts/RefresherContext.jsx`, `src/reducers/refresherReducer.js`) for forbidden import patterns — html2canvas / jspdf / pdf-lib via 6 regex variants covering both `from '...'` and `require('...')` shapes. Smoke-tested ✅ on current tree — zero forbidden imports. **(7)** Tests (4 files, 76 new tests): `refresherReducer.test.js` (19 tests — initial state 2 + REFRESHER_HYDRATED 5 incl. failure-path-still-ready + REFRESHER_CONFIG_REPLACED 5 incl. wrong-id defensive + REFRESHER_BATCH_APPENDED 7 incl. duplicate-batchId-drop with config-still-updated); `useRefresherPersistence.test.js` (5 tests — parallel-reads on mount + dispatch shape + isReady transitions + failure-path-still-ready + cancellation guard via blocked Promise + post-unmount); `useRefresherView.test.js` (28 tests — initial state 5 incl. malformed-JSON fallback + non-array filter coercion + invalid-sort coercion / setFilter 4 / setSort 3 / setShowSuppressed 3 / resetView 2); `RefresherContext.test.jsx` (24 tests — Provider basics 4 + outside-Provider throw 1 + patchConfig W-URC-1 path 2 incl. error propagation + setCardVisibility 1 + setClassSuppressed 1 + recordPrintBatch 1 + 6 selector-helper coverage including getStaleCards diverging-hash detection). **All 76/76 green.** Full PRF + persistence + reducer + hooks + context scope: **352/352 green across 15 test files.** **Doctrine choices established:** (a) Post-write update pattern (UI handler awaits writer → dispatch with returned record) chosen over EAL's per-slice diff-write because writers.js validates field-ownership; per-slice diff-write would bypass writer validation. (e) Provider helper recordPrintBatch composes updatedConfig client-side from existing reducer state + new lastExportAt instead of re-reading IDB — single dispatch updates both slices atomically at reducer level. **Prior update (superseded, kept for provenance — 2026-04-26 earlier):** (**Exploit Anchor Library — Phase 6 Stream D B3 Context/reducer/persistence-hook SHIPPED (Option B).** Session 13 closes the state-management layer mirroring MPMF S9 G5-B1 EntitlementContext pattern. **4 new files + 1 extended + 3 new test files; net 63 new tests; total anchorLibrary tests 437 green** (374 from S12 + 63 from S13). **Files shipped:** **(1)** `src/constants/anchorLibraryConstants.js` extended with `ANCHOR_LIBRARY_ACTIONS` frozen enum (8 actions: ANCHOR_LIBRARY_HYDRATED + OBSERVATION_CAPTURED/DELETED + DRAFT_UPDATED/CLEARED + ANCHOR_OVERRIDDEN + PRIMITIVE_VALIDITY_UPDATED + ENROLLMENT_TOGGLED) + `ENROLLMENT_STATES` enum + `VALID_ENROLLMENT_STATES` array + `initialAnchorLibraryState` (5 frozen empty dicts + enrollment defaulting to `'not-enrolled'` per Q1-A red line #1 opt-in + schemaVersion `'1.0.0'`) + `ANCHOR_LIBRARY_STATE_SCHEMA` for createValidatedReducer top-level type checks. **(2)** `src/reducers/anchorLibraryReducer.js` — pure raw reducer wrapped in `createValidatedReducer`; 8 case branches with `arrayToDict` (tolerates non-array hydration payloads) + `removeKey` (returns same dict ref when key absent for render-stability); immutable spread updates throughout; defensive returns same-state when payload missing required fields (no `id` / no `handId` / invalid enrollment state); ANCHOR_OVERRIDDEN + PRIMITIVE_VALIDITY_UPDATED merge updated fields onto existing record (caller passes full record per W-EA-3 / W-PP-2 contract; merge handles common case of "just changed status + timestamp"); DRAFT_UPDATED auto-attaches deterministic `draft:<handId>` id when caller doesn't provide one; ENROLLMENT_TOGGLED rejects invalid state values via `VALID_ENROLLMENT_STATES.includes` check. **(3)** `src/contexts/AnchorLibraryContext.jsx` — `AnchorLibraryProvider` receiving state + dispatch as props from useAppState (Phase 6+ wiring); composes `useAnchorLibraryPersistence` internally to hydrate IDB state on mount; exposes 8 selector helpers via `useCallback`+`useMemo` for render-stability — `selectAllAnchors()` (red line #6 flat-access — returns ALL statuses including retired/suppressed/candidate), `selectActiveAnchors()` (live matcher pre-filter), `selectAnchorsByStatus(status)` (Anchor Library status-filter + retirement journey panels), `selectObservationsByHand(handId)` (capture-modal inline list, **chronological DESC sort newest first**), `selectDraftForHand(handId)` (capture-modal resume-banner check; returns null when no draft), `selectAllPrimitives()` (Calibration Dashboard primitives panel), `selectPrimitivesByStyle(style)` (mirrors `getPrimitivesByStyle` IDB query in-memory — Nit→PP-01/04/07/08, Fish→PP-03/05/06/08), `isEnrolled()` (capture-modal Incognito toggle gating + Calibration Dashboard enrollment-banner); `useAnchorLibrary` consumer hook throws helpful error `must be used within an AnchorLibraryProvider` outside Provider. **(4)** `src/hooks/useAnchorLibraryPersistence.js` — mount-hydration via `Promise.all` over the 4 wrapper getAlls (`getAllAnchors` + `getAllObservations` + `getAllDrafts` + `getAllPrimitives` — parallel reads; faster than sequential; safe because wrappers are independent stores) → single `ANCHOR_LIBRARY_HYDRATED` dispatch with full payload (reducer bulk-loads in one render); `enrollment: undefined` defers to settings store / persisted user preference (Phase 6+ wires; for now defaults to not-enrolled); marks `isReady: true` after hydration including failure path (app remains usable on IDB error per usability principle inherited from useEntitlementPersistence); 400ms-debounced per-slice diff-write — previous-state ref compared to new state via `useRef`, only changed slices written via appropriate wrapper (`putAnchor` / `putObservation` / `putDraft` / `putPrimitive`); for drafts and observations slices, **removed-key detection drives `deleteDraft` / `deleteObservation` calls** — DRAFT_CLEARED action removes key from dict → hook detects via `!(id in newState.drafts)` check + extracts handId from `draft:<handId>` id format + calls `deleteDraft(handId)` wrapper; pre-hydration write guard via `hasHydratedRef` prevents overwriting IDB with empty defaults before actual records load. **Tests (3 files, 63 total):** `anchorLibraryReducer.test.js` (29 tests — initial state validation 4 + ANCHOR_LIBRARY_HYDRATED 4 + OBSERVATION_CAPTURED 5 + OBSERVATION_DELETED 3 + DRAFT_UPDATED 5 + DRAFT_CLEARED 2 + ANCHOR_OVERRIDDEN 3 + PRIMITIVE_VALIDITY_UPDATED 2 + ENROLLMENT_TOGGLED 4 [valid + invalid + roundtrip + ENROLLMENT_STATES export] + unknown-action defensive 1); `AnchorLibraryContext.test.jsx` (22 tests — Provider rendering 4 + outside-provider throw 1 + selectAllAnchors flat-access 2 + selectActiveAnchors filter 1 + selectAnchorsByStatus 1 + selectObservationsByHand chronological-DESC 2 + selectDraftForHand 2 + selectAllPrimitives + selectPrimitivesByStyle 3 + isEnrolled 2; mocks useAnchorLibraryPersistence to isolate context behavior from IDB); `useAnchorLibraryPersistence.test.js` (12 tests — parallel hydration 1 + ANCHOR_LIBRARY_HYDRATED dispatch shape 1 + isReady transitions 2 [happy + failure-path-still-ready] + pre-hydration write guard via blocked Promise 1 + debounced-write-after-400ms via fake timers 1 + per-action wrappers: putObservation on observation change 1 + deleteObservation on key removal 1 + putDraft on draft change 1 + deleteDraft on draft key removal 1 + putPrimitive on primitive change 1 + per-slice independence: observation-only-change does not re-write unchanged anchors slice 1; mocks 4 persistence wrapper modules + uses fake timers for debounce verification). **All 63 new tests green.** Full suite **7981/7985** — 4 failures: pre-existing precisionAudit flake (drillContent/, documented since 2026-04-22) + pre-existing gameTreeHelpers parallel-execution flake (cross-test-IDB-deletion race like postflopDrillsStorage) + parallel MPMF G5-B2 TelemetryConsentContext-missing-test schema-validation failure (their incomplete work; my AnchorLibraryContext does have a test) + parallel migrationV21 tests not yet aligned with their own implementation (telemetryConsent seed shape mismatch in test fixtures). **None are regressions from S13 work.** **Coordination note:** between S12 and S13 multiple parallel sessions shipped: MPMF G5-B2 telemetry foundation (DB_VERSION 20→21 + telemetryConsent store + migrateV21) and PRF-G5-WR closed (3-writer registry + CI-grep enforcement; PRF G5-MIG / SL / ST / WR all complete now). PRF S13 handled the cross-cutting test edits for the v21 bump including my `anchorLibraryStores.test.js` DB_VERSION assertion (their floor-pattern adjustment preserves my v19 store intent). Zero file conflicts with my S13 work — I touched only EAL-namespace files (constants extension + reducer + context + hook + 3 test files). **Design choices this session:** (a) **Per-slice diff-write** in persistence hook avoids re-writing all 4 stores on every dispatch — at the seed-anchor scale (4 anchors / ≤100 obs / ≤10 drafts / 8 primitives) this matters less, but Phase 8 library expansion (10-50 anchors) makes it meaningful + keeps the pattern future-proof. (b) **Removed-key detection** for drafts and observations slices is the load-bearing piece — DRAFT_CLEARED / OBSERVATION_DELETED actions remove keys from dict; without removed-key detection, the canonical IDB record would persist after the user discards a draft or deletes an observation. The detection compares previous and current dict keysets via `for (const id of Object.keys(prev))` + `if (!(id in current))`. (c) **Anchors and primitives slices have no delete actions** by design — per W-EA-3 retirement uses status-update not delete (red line #6 flat-access; retired anchors stay visible in library); per W-PP-2 primitive validity updates merge into the record (W-PP-3 owner override is Phase 8). So the persistence hook only handles delete-detection on drafts + observations, not on anchors + primitives. (d) **`useCallback` on every selector** — could potentially be optimized to a single useMemo returning all selectors but the per-callback approach is cleaner and React's useCallback dependency-array stability handles re-render avoidance. Mirror of EntitlementContext pattern. (e) **Mocked persistence in context tests** — context tests don't need real IDB to verify selector behavior; isolating concerns lets context tests run fast (~700ms for 22 tests) while the persistence hook gets dedicated coverage with mocks of all 4 wrapper modules for fine-grained behavioral assertions. **B3 state-management layer COMPLETE.** Phase 6 Stream D status: foundation ✅ (S10) + IDB ✅ (S11) + persistence wrappers ✅ (S12) + reducer/context/hook ✅ (S13). **Next session direction:** AppRoot wiring (3 small file edits: `useAppState.js` adds `useReducer(anchorLibraryReducer, initialAnchorLibraryState)` + `AppProviders.jsx` adds `<AnchorLibraryProvider>` in the provider stack + `contexts/index.js` exports useAnchorLibrary + AnchorLibraryProvider; ~30 LOC + integration test verifying full state→IDB→read-back round-trip with no mocks) — once wired, the capture flow becomes end-to-end testable. Then **Option C (capture React components):** AnchorObservationButton (Section G entry ≥44×44) + AnchorObservationModal (8-tag enum chip grid + custom-tag input + street/action pickers + 280-char note + Incognito toggle primary-visible per red line #9) + AnchorObservationList (chronological DESC; selector wired) + useAnchorObservationCapture orchestrator hook (composes captureObservation pure writer + useAnchorLibrary dispatch + dirty-draft-confirm-sheet logic) + useAnchorObservationDraft sidecar (400ms debounce on edit → DRAFT_UPDATED dispatch) + ReviewPanel.jsx Section G integration → visible owner value. Estimated 2-3 sessions for full capture flow. Handoff: `.claude/handoffs/exploit-anchor-library-session13.md`.)

New robust pattern: assert invariants not absolute version numbers; future MPMF/EAL bumps don't require PRF test edits. **(1)** `src/utils/printableRefresher/writers.js` — 3 writer functions per WRITERS.md v1.0: `writeConfigPreferences(patch)` (W-URC-1 read-merge-put orchestration over printPreferences/notifications/lastExportAt; rejects cardVisibility/suppressedClasses/unknown top-level keys via I-WR-3 segregation with helpful "Use writeCardVisibility / writeSuppressedClass" error messages; rejects `printPreferences.includeCodex: true` per AP-PRF-09 + red line #16 with explicit Phase-2+ deferral cite to PRF-P2-PE; rejects unknown printPreferences/notifications nested keys with valid-keys hint; rejects non-string-or-null lastExportAt; preserves `id: 'singleton'` through merge; returns merged singleton record); `writeCardVisibility({cardId, visibility})` (W-URC-2a immediate single-tap action; rejects empty cardId + invalid visibility outside `{default, hidden, pinned}`; **special semantics: `'default'` removes the entry from cardVisibility map** to avoid unbounded map growth as users toggle through pin/hide/back-to-default — selectors handle missing entries via fallback to default; hide-then-pin overwrites last-write; preserves other cards); `writeSuppressedClass({classId, suppress, confirmed, ownerInitiated})` (W-URC-2b immediate; rejects empty classId + non-boolean suppress; **suppress=true requires `options.confirmed === true`** at writer boundary as defense-in-depth against direct API calls bypassing SuppressConfirmModal per red line #13 deliberate-suppression — error message cites the red line; **suppress=false requires `options.ownerInitiated === true`** at writer boundary per AP-PRF-05 refusal of programmatic un-suppress nudges — no "reconsider this card?" cross-card surfacer permitted; idempotent suppress no-duplicate; un-suppress not-suppressed is no-op; preserves other suppressed classes); `writePrintBatch(payload)` (W-URC-3 batch creation per red line #15 owner-initiated only; generates `batchId` via `crypto.randomUUID()` with Math.random RFC4122-v4 fallback for environments without it — acceptable since IDB keypath uniqueness here is not security-critical, batches identify records not authenticate them; rejects empty cardIds + empty printedAt + empty engineVersion + empty appVersion + null perCardSnapshots + non-string-or-null label; **I-WR-6 perCardSnapshots completeness** validates keys MUST equal cardIds set 1:1 — rejects size mismatch + extraneous keys + missing snapshots + non-string contentHash + non-string version per snapshot; warns dev-mode `console.warn` on `printedAt > +1 day` future without rejecting — owner may be backdating future-print reminder; **post-write side effect invokes `writeConfigPreferences({lastExportAt: printedAt})`** implementing WRITERS.md note on lastExportAt single-ownership through W-URC-1 even though W-URC-3 triggers it; returns `{batchId, record}` so caller can surface confirmation toast). **(2)** `src/utils/printableRefresher/__tests__/writers.test.js` — 55 tests across 7 describes: W-URC-1 happy-path 6 + I-WR-3 rejects 5 + AP-PRF-09 includeCodex 2 + input-shape rejects 5; W-URC-2a happy-path 5 + input rejects 4; W-URC-2b happy-path 5 + confirm/ownerInitiated guards 4 + input rejects 2; W-URC-3 happy-path 5 (incl. **post-write side effect lastExportAt updated** + **buildDefaultRefresherConfig defaults preserved across W-URC-3 lastExportAt update** — only lastExportAt changes byte-equal-rest) + I-WR-6 rejects 4 + input rejects 7; writers integration multi-writer-coexist 1 (full lifecycle: config-pref + visibility + suppression + print-batch all coexist in singleton + lastExportAt updated by W-URC-3 side effect). **All 55/55 green.** **(3)** `scripts/check-refresher-writers.sh` (executable bash CI-grep gate per WRITERS.md §I-WR-1 + §I-WR-5): Check 1 — I-WR-1 enumeration scans `src/` for any `(put|delete)(...)` call referencing userRefresherConfig/printBatches store names + filters out ALLOWED_WRITER_FILES (writers.js / writers.test.js / refresherStore.js / refresherStore.test.js / refresherMigration.test.js / migrations.js — migration's seed put() at upgrade time is legitimate and registered); Smoke-tested on current tree — passes ✅ "PRF writer registry check: OK / I-WR-1 enumeration: all put/delete calls registered / I-WR-5 append-only: zero printBatches deletes outside permitted scope." Wiring into smart-test-runner.sh + CI pipeline deferred to PRF-G5-HK or dedicated CI-wiring session. **Doctrine choices established:** (a) Writers throw synchronously on validation failure — callers (UI handlers) try/catch around writer calls; useRefresherConfig hook (PRF-G5-HK next session) will translate errors into reducer-state error fields the UI surfaces as toasts; don't unify writer error handling at writer level — keep explicit at call-sites for testability. (b) `lastExportAt` shared-write pattern is two-sequential-IDB-transactions in production (atomicity not guaranteed across a crash between W-URC-3 batch-put and W-URC-1 lastExportAt-put) — acceptable because fields are independent semantically + next W-URC-1 call would update lastExportAt anyway + missing lastExportAt update doesn't break selectStaleCards or any read path. Documented in writers.js. (c) `'default'` visibility removes entry from map — keeping `cardVisibility[cardId] === 'default'` would grow map unboundedly; selectors fallback to default for missing entries so read-side contract preserved. (d) `crypto.randomUUID()` fallback acceptable for batchId — fallback uses Math.random for v4 shape; collision probability astronomically low across few batches per owner; NOT used for authentication or signing. If future audit flags, swap to `nanoid` (~1KB) or Node crypto polyfill. (e) **DB_VERSION test pattern shifts from absolute-value to invariant-assertion**: `≥ 18` (spec floor) + `≥ 20` (PRF claim preserved). Robust to future bumps; v20→v21 (MPMF) and v20→? (future PRF Phase 2+) cases both pass without re-editing PRF tests. (f) Multi-writer-coexist integration test is LOAD-BEARING sanity contract — exercises all 4 writer functions in sequence + asserts singleton state + W-URC-3 side effect; if any single writer's contract breaks, this test fails. (g) CI-grep filter MUST include `migrations.js` — migration's seed put() at upgrade time is legitimate; without filter, CI-grep falsely flags as unregistered writer. (h) Dev script wiring into smart-test-runner.sh deferred — one-line script edit; can land at PRF-G5-HK or dedicated CI-wiring session. **Phase 5 sequencing post-S13:** PRF-G5-CI ✓ + PRF-G5-MIG ✓ + PRF-G5-SL ✓ + PRF-G5-ST ✓ + PRF-G5-WR ✓ → **PRF-G5-HK NEXT-unblocked**: `src/hooks/useRefresherConfig.js` IDB-backed singleton config hook with 400ms-debounced writes via W-URC-1 mirroring useAssumptionPersistence + useEntitlementPersistence patterns; `src/hooks/useRefresherView.js` localStorage-backed UI state pure-no-IDB; `src/contexts/RefresherContext.jsx` provider; `src/reducers/refresherReducer.js` with action validation; `scripts/check-refresher-bundle.sh` per print-css-doctrine.md forbidding html2canvas/jspdf/pdf-lib imports in PRF namespace.
