**Prior update (superseded, kept for provenance — 2026-04-26 earlier):** (**Printable Refresher (PRF) — PRF-G5-SL + PRF-G5-ST CLOSED (selectors + store CRUD wrappers).** Continues PRF-G5-CI (S1-S4 / 4 commits 2026-04-25) + PRF-G5-MIG (S11 / commit `f869141`). The persistence + selector wiring step splits into 4 sub-deliverables: PRF-G5-SL (selectors) ✓ + PRF-G5-ST (store wrappers) ✓ ship this session; PRF-G5-WR (writer registry + CI-grep) is next; PRF-G5-HK (React hooks + bundle-grep CI) BLOCKED by WR. **S12 deliverables (4 new files + 4 BACKLOG row updates):** **(1)** `src/utils/printableRefresher/refresherSelectors.js` — 6 selectors per `selectors.md` v1.0 + `annotateCard()` helper. `selectAllCards` (base read; never filters; never hides — used for catalog "Show suppressed" full view + partition source set). `selectActiveCards` (default catalog read; excludes hidden + class-suppressed). `selectPinnedCards` (visibility === 'pinned' subset; trusts writer-layer pin-un-hide coupling). `selectSuppressedCards` (hidden OR class-suppressed; inverse of active; partition constraint asserted). `selectCardsForBatchPrint(selectedIds)` (selectedIds filtered to active — defense-in-depth against UI bugs allowing selection of suppressed cards). `selectStaleCards(printBatches)` (active cards whose contentHash differs from most-recent print snapshot; sorts batches by printedAt DESC internally so callers can pass unsorted; cards never printed not stale; hidden+suppressed cards excluded — no laminate to be stale; matching hash → current; diverging hash → stale with isStale:true + currentHash + printedHash + printedAt + batchId + batchLabel). `annotateCard(card, config)` returns `{...card, visibility, classSuppressed, isStale: null, staleSinceBatch: null}`; rejects unrecognized visibility values back to 'default' (defense-in-depth against corrupted IDB). **(2)** `src/utils/printableRefresher/__tests__/refresherSelectors.test.js` — 39 tests covering all 6 selectors + 4 state-clear-asymmetry roundtrip tests (PRF-G5-SL-ROUNDTRIP-PIN/HIDE/SUPPRESS/UNSUPPRESS) including the canonical un-suppress zero-data-loss proof (pin 3 cards → suppress class → un-suppress class → all 3 still pinned via 3-snapshot writer-state evolution simulation) + PRF-G5-SL-PARTITION (active ∪ suppressed === all, intersection empty across mixed visibility+suppression state) + 2 purity guardrails (no-mutation of inputs, deterministic equal-output). 39/39 green. **(3)** `src/utils/persistence/refresherStore.js` — 6 IDB CRUD wrappers: `getRefresherConfig()` (lazy-creates default if missing — defense-in-depth for corrupted-DB recovery), `putRefresherConfig(record)` (throws on null/missing-id/wrong-id; validates `record.id === 'singleton'`), `putPrintBatch(record)` (throws on null/empty-batchId/empty-printedAt; does NOT enforce append-only at IDB layer per architectural separation — that's writer-layer responsibility), `getPrintBatch(batchId)`, `getAllPrintBatches()` (returns sorted by printedAt DESC at wrapper level so callers don't repeat), `getPrintBatchesForCard(cardId)` (filtered + DESC-sorted). Pure data layer; mirrors EAL `anchorObservationsStore.js` pattern with synchronous input-validation throws + IDB-error log/propagate. **(4)** `src/utils/persistence/__tests__/refresherStore.test.js` — 21 tests: singleton round-trip with mutated colorMode+cardsPerSheet + lazy-default-on-missing-record + 4 input-validation rejects + only-1-record-after-N-puts (id-keyed put is upsert); printBatch round-trip + null-on-missing + 4 input-validations; getAllPrintBatches empty + DESC-sorted with 3 out-of-order fixtures + field-preservation end-to-end with label/cardIds/perCardSnapshots; getPrintBatchesForCard filtered (3-batch fixture, 2 contain card A, 2 contain card B, 1 contains both) + empty-when-not-printed + empty-cardId-rejects; I-WR-5 append-only 5-record persistence + same-batchId-overwrites note (UI must not call this path; W-URC-3 generates fresh UUIDs). 21/21 green. **Doctrine choices established:** (a) Selectors are pure with no IDB reads — all state flows in via inputs, separating I/O from logic; matches `selectors.md` §Memoization contract for shallow-equal memoization. (b) `selectStaleCards` sorts batches internally as defense — callers can pass unsorted/partial arrays without breaking logic (cost is one Array.sort per render at expected batch counts in low dozens, negligible). (c) `annotateCard` rejects unrecognized visibility values — corrupted IDB shouldn't crash render code. (d) `getRefresherConfig` lazy-creates default on missing-record — corrupted-DB return-null preferable to crash; the writer layer's first put() would restore singleton state. (e) `putPrintBatch` does NOT enforce append-only at IDB layer — that's writer-layer (W-URC-3) responsibility per WRITERS.md I-WR-5; production code must never call this primitive with a duplicate batchId since W-URC-3 generates fresh UUIDs via `crypto.randomUUID()`. (f) State-clear-asymmetry roundtrip tests are LOAD-BEARING for R-8.1 doctrine compliance; the un-suppress canonical proof (3-snapshot pin/suppress/un-suppress cycle preserves pinned-id set byte-for-byte) is the explicit contract that `cardVisibility` is never cleared by class-suppression writes. (g) `selectCardsForBatchPrint` defense-in-depth dropping is intentional — even if UI strictly prevents selecting a suppressed card, selector excludes it from print set; caller (PrintConfirmationModal) compares lengths to surface "1 selected card was suppressed + excluded from print" warning. (h) No batch-deletion path in `refresherStore.js` — I-WR-5 invariant; CI-grep at PRF-G5-WR will assert zero `.delete()` calls against `printBatches`. **Governance:** 4 BACKLOG rows added/updated — PRF-G5-SL + PRF-G5-ST flipped to COMPLETE with full accept-criteria detail + 39+21=60 test breakdown; PRF-G5-WR (NEXT, gated on SL+ST green ✓) and PRF-G5-HK (BLOCKED by WR) added as placeholders. Section header updated: "Gate 5 IN PROGRESS — PRF-G5-CI + PRF-G5-MIG + PRF-G5-SL + PRF-G5-ST CLOSED 2026-04-26." **PRF-G5-WR next deliverables:** `src/utils/printableRefresher/writers.js` exporting 3 writers (W-URC-1 `writeConfigPreferences(patch)` 400ms-debounced via hook layer with field-ownership validator rejecting cardVisibility/suppressedClasses + includeCodex:true Phase-1 enforcement / W-URC-2 `writeCardVisibility({cardId, visibility})` + `writeSuppressedClass({classId, suppress, ownerInitiated})` immediate with `options.confirmed === true` defense-in-depth at suppress-writer + `options.ownerInitiated === true` at un-suppress-writer + rejects printPreferences/notifications/lastExportAt patches / W-URC-3 `writePrintBatch(payload)` rejects empty cardIds + perCardSnapshots key-mismatch with cardIds (I-WR-6 completeness) + warns on printedAt > +1 day + `crypto.randomUUID()` batchId generation + invokes W-URC-1 `writeConfigPreferences({lastExportAt: printedAt})` as final post-write side effect) + `writers.test.js` covering each validator's reject cases + `scripts/check-refresher-writers.sh` CI-grep mirroring `scripts/check-sidebar-writers.sh` pattern. **Parallel session coordination:** No parallel-session activity between S11 commit and this S12 commit. (b) Singleton seed via in-flight upgrade transaction (matching EAL precedent) lands atomically with store creation; idempotent put() handles partial-failure replay; don't use post-upgrade transaction (races with upgrade transaction). (e) `printBatches` empty at create per I-WR-5 — first record on first owner print confirmation; "default batch" seeding would violate append-only + create phantom batch the staleness logic might mis-index. (c) Cross-wrapper integration test verifies the two-transaction discipline of the capture-modal Save: `putObservation` then `deleteDraft` as separate IDB transactions (intentional — atomic-failure recovery is "draft survives, no canonical observation" or "canonical exists, no draft" — both are safe states; only "neither succeeded" or "both succeeded" matter, and the unsafe middle state is impossible since each transaction is independent). 5 new STORE_NAME exports (`EXPLOIT_ANCHORS_STORE_NAME` / `ANCHOR_OBSERVATIONS_STORE_NAME` / `ANCHOR_OBSERVATION_DRAFTS_STORE_NAME` / `ANCHOR_CANDIDATES_STORE_NAME` / `PERCEPTION_PRIMITIVES_STORE_NAME`). **(3)** `src/utils/persistence/migrations.js` added `migrateV19(db, transaction)` — creates 5 stores per schema-delta §5.1 with all indexes (exploitAnchors keypath `id` + 7 indexes including `lastUpdated` on `evidence.lastUpdated` + multi-style `tier`/`polarity`/`status`/`schemaVersion`; anchorObservations keypath `id` + 5 indexes including `origin` for AP-08 signal-separation queries; anchorObservationDrafts sidecar keypath `id` + handId/updatedAt for cleanup queries; anchorCandidates Phase-2-empty with status/ownerPromotedAt/archetypeName indexes; perceptionPrimitives keypath `id` + multi-entry index on `appliesToStyles` enabling style-keyed primitive lookups + `lastUpdated`); seeds perceptionPrimitives via `seedPerceptionPrimitives` in same transaction so atomic with store creation; orchestrator wired `if (oldVersion < 19) migrateV19(db, transaction)` after migrateV18 hook. **(4)** `src/utils/persistence/__tests__/anchorLibraryStores.test.js` (NEW; 31 tests in 7 describe blocks): DB_VERSION at v19 (1); fresh-install creates all 5 EAL stores with correct keypaths and all enumerated indexes (5); perceptionPrimitives seeded with exactly 8 records matching PP-01..PP-08 ids + content checks PP-01 references Nit+TAG+inverse PP-03 / PP-04 references off-script / PP-08 universal-applies-to-all-4-styles + every record has Beta(1,1) prior + sampleSize 0 + 0.95 CI level + ISO8601 lastUpdated + dependentAnchorCount=0 (8); Phase 1 stores start empty exploitAnchors/anchorObservations/anchorObservationDrafts/anchorCandidates (4); idempotency re-open preserves 8 primitives no duplication + 5 stores still present (2; EAL-G5-SI partial coverage); v18 stores untouched additive-only (subscription/players/hands/villainAssumptions all preserved) (4); CRUD round-trip put-then-get on each of 5 EAL stores (5); multiEntry index query verification fetching by Nit returns PP-01/04/07/08 + by Fish returns PP-03/05/06/08 (2). **(5)** `src/utils/persistence/__tests__/database.test.js` updated: "creates all 12 stores" → "creates all 17 stores"; +5 EAL-store contains-checks; storeNames.length 12 → 17. **(6)** `src/utils/persistence/__tests__/subscriptionStore.test.js` patched: DB_VERSION assertion `=== 18` → `>= 18` (subscription store is correctly migrated within v18→v19 chain; intent preserved with comment explaining EAL bumped DB_VERSION per dynamic-target rule). **Total tests added this session: 31 anchorLibraryStores + 5 database.test contains-checks** (other anchorLibrary 291 from S10 unchanged). **Anchor library tests including persistence: 322 green** (291 + 31). Full suite **7674/7675** — same pre-existing precisionAudit flake; zero new regressions from S11 once subscriptionStore DB_VERSION assertion was patched (initial run had 2 fails: precisionAudit flake + subscriptionStore.DB_VERSION-must-be-18; the latter resolved by patching the assertion to `>= 18` since MPMF's intent was "subscription store ships at v18", not "DB_VERSION will never exceed 18"). **Coordination note (gate4-p3-decisions §2 dynamic-target):** v18 was claimed by MPMF S9 G5-B1 (subscription store, shipped 2026-04-25 earlier today — see prior STATUS update for full MPMF context). EAL bumped to v19 per the rule `Math.max(currentVersion+1, targetVersion)` resolving from `currentVersion=18, targetVersion=18 → max(19, 18) = 19`. Future migrations must read `DB_VERSION` constant + bump dynamically; do not hardcode v20 etc. **Design choices this session:** (1) `anchorObservationDrafts` is a separate IDB store (not keypath-namespaced within `anchorObservations`) per S10 handoff prefigured rationale — separation gives index isolation (draft cursors don't scan canonical observations) + simplifies post-Save cleanup (delete from drafts is a separate transaction from the canonical observation write). (2) `seedPerceptionPrimitives` uses `put` not `add` for idempotency under partial-failure-recovery (re-running migration overwrites with same content; safer than throwing on duplicate-id from prior incomplete run). (3) migrate hook seeds via the in-flight upgrade transaction (`transaction.objectStore(storeName)`) ensuring seed atomicity with store creation — if seed fails, store creation rolls back and migration retries cleanly on next open. (4) `multiEntry: true` on `appliesToStyles` index enables `idx.getAll('Nit')` to return all 4 Nit-applicable primitives without loading all 8 records — important for Phase 6 surface filtering (anchor-library style-filter, calibration-dashboard primitives-by-style queries). (5) `perceptionPrimitiveSeed.js` lives in `src/utils/anchorLibrary/` not `src/constants/` because it bundles authored-content data with a behavior function (`buildSeedRecord` + `seedPerceptionPrimitives`); pure constants without behavior live in `src/constants/`. **Phase 6 B3 IDB layer is unblocked** for AnchorLibraryContext + persistence hook + capture modal React components. Recommended next session direction: `useAnchorObservationCapture` hook + `useAnchorObservationDraft` hook + simple `subscriptionStore`-style `anchorObservationsStore.js` CRUD module — mirrors MPMF S9 G5-B1 pattern of "persistence module + reducer + context + hook" but scoped to capture flow only (not the full Anchor Library yet). Handoff: `.claude/handoffs/exploit-anchor-library-session11.md`.)

(b) Tag normalizer separates ASCII-strict policy (only [a-z0-9-]) from rich-text via documented diacritic limitation — keeps the kebab format clean for IDB indexing without breaking on common copy-paste. (c) Capture writer is **pure** (no IDB call, no toast dispatch, no state mutation) — the React layer owns side effects. This separation makes the writer trivially unit-testable and lets Phase 6 Stream D React layer compose without owning invariant enforcement. (d) `contributesToCalibration` 4-way decision tree (`not-enrolled forces false` > `explicit false wins` > `undefined → default true when enrolled` > `truthy non-true falls through to default`) is structurally Q2-A + I-WR-5 + I-WR-6 in one place — not spread across UI + reducer + writer. Single source of truth. **Prior update (superseded, kept for provenance — 2026-04-25 earlier):** **Exploit Anchor Library — Phase 5 Stream E Commit 4 SHIPPED — math layer COMPLETE.** Session 9 closed the Stream E math layer with `primitiveValidity.js` + 47 tests. Three responsibilities in one pure module: (1) **Tier-2 Beta-Binomial posterior updater** — `updatePrimitiveValidity(primitive, firingEvent)` performs the standard Beta-Binomial conjugate update (`Beta(α, β) + supportingEvent → Beta(α+w, β)`, weight `w` clamped to `[0, 1]`). Posterior `pointEstimate` is the new mean `α/(α+β)`; credible interval at 95% level uses normal approximation `mean ± 1.96 × sqrt(variance)` clamped to `[0, 1]`. Supporting/non-supporting count tracked exactly via `supportsCount` accumulator (back-derived from `pointEstimate × sampleSize` for primitives written before this module existed — one-time bootstrap; subsequent updates store exactly). `applyFiringBatch(primitive, events)` reduces over an event array. Beta math is **module-local** — no import from `exploitEngine/bayesianConfidence` to preserve the I-AE-CIRC-1 inheritance from `assumptionEngine/CLAUDE.md` (anchor library does not depend on exploit engine). Normal-approximation choice is fail-safe direction (slightly wider CI than exact Beta CDF inversion → harder to fire invalidation → more conservative auto-retire posture); Phase 6+ may swap to exact Beta CDF if precision becomes load-bearing. (2) **Cross-anchor invalidation ripple computation** per schema-delta §3.3.1 — `evaluatePrimitiveStatus(primitive, options)` classifies primitive as `load-bearing` (CI fully ≥ threshold 0.5) / `at-risk` (CI spans threshold) / `invalidated` (CI fully < threshold). `computeRipple(primitive, dependentAnchors, options)` returns the proposed cross-anchor penalty set when primitive transitions INTO `invalidated` — each dependent anchor's `quality.composite` multiplied by `penaltyFactor` (default 0.85 per §3.3.1). Ripple is **idempotent** — does not re-fire when transitionFrom is already `invalidated`. Conservative default (`transitionFrom: null`) fires when current status is invalidated. **Multi-primitive anchors** (anchors referencing both this primitive and others) ARE penalized — the ripple fires per-primitive-invalidation independently. **Caller (Phase 6 reducer)** applies the ripple updates atomically in a single IDB transaction per I-WR-3 — this module returns proposed updates without mutating; atomicity test target is EAL-G5-CA. **Anchor not auto-retired** by ripple — only `quality.composite` degraded; the anchor remains `active` with weakened composite, and the surface layer can flag it via the dashboard. **No automatic recovery direction** — if primitive's data later flips back to load-bearing, Phase 5 implementation does NOT auto-restore the composite (Phase 8 concern; recovery requires audit-trail considerations). (3) **I-EAL-9 dependent-anchor-count invariant rebuild** — `rebuildDependentAnchorCount(primitive, allAnchors)` recomputes the canonical count `count(anchors where perceptionPrimitiveIds includes this.id)`. Caller invokes whenever the anchor list changes (every anchor write per WRITERS.md I-WR-2). Pure function; immutability verified in tests. **Public API:** 7 exports added to index.js — `updatePrimitiveValidity`, `applyFiringBatch`, `evaluatePrimitiveStatus`, `computeRipple`, `rebuildDependentAnchorCount`, `PRIMITIVE_LOAD_BEARING_THRESHOLD` (0.5), `DEFAULT_PENALTY_FACTOR` (0.85). **47 new tests** organized in 7 describe blocks: Beta math (10 tests — prior baseline / one-supporting-shifts-toward-1 / one-non-supporting-shifts-toward-0 / 50-event convergence / mixed proportion match / weight in (0,1] respected / weight clamped on out-of-range / observedAt preserved in lastUpdated / immutability / throw-on-missing-supportsClaim / throw-on-null-primitive); credible-interval bounds (3 — always [0,1] / shrinks with sample size / point-estimate-inside-CI); applyFiringBatch (3 — in-order / empty / throw-on-non-array); evaluatePrimitiveStatus (8 — load-bearing CI-above / at-risk CI-spans / invalidated CI-below / lower-exactly-at-threshold load-bearing / upper-exactly-at-threshold at-risk [strict < rule] / custom threshold / missing-CI-default-load-bearing / constants exported); computeRipple (12 — load-bearing no-fire / at-risk no-fire / load-bearing→invalidated fires + correct penalty / idempotent invalidated→invalidated no-fire / null transitionFrom fires conservatively / only-referencing-anchors-penalized / multi-primitive anchor-penalized / skip-malformed-composite / custom-penaltyFactor / throw-on-out-of-range-penalty / throw-on-non-array-anchors / empty-anchors-still-fires-with-status); I-EAL-9 (7 — counts referencing / zero-no-references / zero-empty / immutability / preserves-other-fields / throw-on-null / throw-on-non-array); integration (3 — 50-supporting stays load-bearing / 30-supporting-then-60-non-supporting drives invalidation / PP-04 worst-case 25/25 lands at-risk). **Total anchorLibrary tests: 202 green** (up from 155 in Commit 3; +47 net). Full suite **7350/7351** — same pre-existing precisionAudit flake unchanged; zero new regressions from Commit 4. **Stream E math layer is now CONCEPTUALLY COMPLETE** — schema validation + Tier-1 scenario runner + 4 synthetic villains + 4 Tier-1 scenarios + retirement evaluator + primitive validity all in place. Only Commit 2.5 remains in Stream E: end-to-end producer wiring (replace scenario test stubs with real assumptionEngine integration; requires exploit-deviation coordination on PREDICATE_KEYS extension). Recommended next session direction: (a) Commit 2.5 to close Stream E entirely OR (b) jump ahead to Phase 6 Stream D (IDB v18 migration + 4 surfaces + 13 writers; gated on Stream E being green which it now is at the math layer) since end-to-end producer wiring is technically a Stream E ↔ assumptionEngine integration concern that doesn't block Phase 6 surfaces. Handoff: `.claude/handoffs/exploit-anchor-library-session9.md`.)

**Prior update (superseded, kept for provenance — 2026-04-24 earlier):** (**Exploit Anchor Library — Phase 5 Stream E Commit 3 SHIPPED (retirement evaluator).** Session 8 extended Commits 1+2 with the Tier-3 session-close retirement evaluator per `anchor-retirement.md` journey Variation D. **Files shipped (2 new + 1 updated):** `src/utils/anchorLibrary/retirementEvaluator.js` — pure module, no IO, no side effects; `evaluateAnchorRetirement(anchor, context)` returns `RetirementDecision | null | { skipped: true, reason }`; `evaluateAllAnchors(anchors, context)` returns `{ transitions, skipped, errors }` batch aggregation that one bad entry does not poison. **Two retirement-condition methods:** (1) **credible-interval-overlap** — fires when `ci.lower ≤ gtoBaseline.referenceRate ≤ ci.upper` (observed-rate posterior no longer excludes GTO-balanced baseline). Used by SEED-01 / SEED-03 / SEED-04. (2) **gap-threshold** — fires when `|pointEstimate − referenceRate| ≤ params.gap` for `params.sessions` consecutive session-closes (current + N-1 priors from `context.sessionHistory`). Used by SEED-02 with `{gap: 0.05, sessions: 10}` per seed-02 §7 reasoning (hero's call-EV is sensitive to point estimate, not just CI overlap). Consecutive-session logic sorts history by closedAt DESC and requires every one of N entries to fire — insufficient history returns fired=false with session-count in metrics. **Status-transition rules:** `active → expiring` on first fire + `expiring → retired` on subsequent fire (two-step per seed-01 §7 + journey spec). `candidate / retired / suppressed` all skipped with explicit reason (no auto-transition). **Owner-override durability (red line #3 no-algorithmic-rebuttal):** if `operator.lastOverrideBy === 'owner'` AND `operator.lastOverrideAt` more recent than `evidence.lastUpdated` (ISO8601 parse comparison with malformed-parse fallback treating override as binding — safer default), evaluator skips auto-transition entirely. This makes durable overrides structurally honored at the evaluator layer, not just the UI. **H-N05 session-close boundary:** evaluator is called exactly once per session-close (no mid-session transitions per journey spec) — the boundary is caller-enforced, not enforced inside the evaluator (pure function). `retirementEvaluator.test.js` — **33 new tests** covering: ci-overlap method (CI-above-GTO no-fire / CI-spans-GTO fire / exact-boundary fire / expiring→retired second-fire / missing CI no-fire / missing referenceRate no-fire); gap-threshold method (single-session: gap-exceeds no-fire / gap-at-threshold fire / gap-below-threshold fire; consecutive-session: insufficient-history no-fire / one-prior-session-fails no-fire / all-sessions-fire retires); terminal & no-op status (candidate skipped / retired skipped / suppressed skipped / missing-status-defaults-to-active fires); owner-override durability (recent-override-binds / older-override-does-not / non-owner-override-ignored / missing-evidence-timestamp-treats-override-binding / malformed-timestamp-treats-override-binding); input validation (null/undefined/string anchors rejected / null context rejected / missing retirementCondition no-fire / unknown method no-fire); batch aggregation (transitions + skipped + errors split correctly / null anchors array errors / empty array / one-bad-entry-does-not-poison-batch); integration with authored seed retirementCondition shapes (SEED-01 ci-overlap current state no-fire — divergence still meaningful / SEED-02 gap-threshold shape parses correctly / SEED-04 candidate status always-skipped even if would-fire). `index.js` expanded: 2 new exports (`evaluateAnchorRetirement`, `evaluateAllAnchors`) + Commit 3 banner. **Total anchorLibrary tests: 155 green** (up from 122 in Commit 2). Full suite **7238/7239** — same pre-existing precisionAudit flake unchanged; zero new regressions. **Commit 3 design choices:** (1) pure-module + caller-enforces-session-boundary — evaluator is a scheduled-periodic-task-style function, not a reducer-integrated one; session-close hook in Phase 6 will invoke it once per session-close and apply transitions atomically via W-EA-3 writer (per WRITERS.md). (2) `evaluateAllAnchors` split into transitions/skipped/errors lets caller distinguish "no-op because of durable state" (skipped) from "bad data" (errors) when logging — useful for Phase 6 telemetry. (3) owner-override comparison uses ISO8601 `Date.parse` with fallback to treating-override-as-binding on parse failure — fail-safe direction is preserving owner intent. (4) `candidate` status never auto-transitions even if retirement condition would fire — prevents a failing candidate anchor from silently retiring before owner has a chance to review the PP-04 primitive-validity evidence. (5) Status default is `'active'` when missing — matches VillainAssumption v1.1 default from assumptionEngine; prevents silent no-op on schema-under-construction records. **Commits 2.5 and 4 remain** in Stream E: end-to-end producer wiring (replace scenario test stubs with real assumptionEngine integration) + `primitiveValidity.js` (Tier-2 posterior updater + cross-anchor invalidation atomicity → EAL-G5-CA test target). Handoff: `.claude/handoffs/exploit-anchor-library-session8.md`.)
